
defined_text = {

		localisation_key = Rights_Subject
		trigger = { NOT = { government = republic } }
	}
}

defined_text = {
	name = Rights_Legitimacy
	text = {
		localisation_key = Rights_Meritocracy
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_reform = celestial_empire
				#is_key_equal = { lhs = Pol_Privileges value = 3 }
				has_reform = Yuan_Monarchy
				#is_key_equal = { lhs = Pol_Privileges value = 9 }
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = Rights_HordeUnity
		trigger = {
			is_nomad = yes
		}
	}
	text = {

		trigger = {

		}

defined_text = {
	name = Reqs_CapLearningMinor
	text = { 
		localisation_key = Reqs_CapLearningMinor_G
		trigger = { 
			any_owned_province = {
				culture = ROOT
				OR = {
					has_province_modifier = LN_Minor
					has_province_modifier = LN_Important
					has_province_modifier = LN_Major
				}
			}
		}
	}
	text = { 
		localisation_key = Reqs_CapLearningMinor_R
		trigger = { 
			NOT = { 
				any_owned_province = {
					culture = ROOT
					OR = {
						has_province_modifier = LN_Minor
						has_province_modifier = LN_Important
						has_province_modifier = LN_Major
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
